DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `assets`;
CREATE TABLE `assets` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `equipped_date` date NOT NULL,
  `quantity` int NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `brand` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `usage_type` enum('vehicle','staff') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `vehicle_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `staff_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `note` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `is_active` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `created_by` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_by` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `deleted_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `assets_vehicle_id_foreign` (`vehicle_id`),
  KEY `assets_staff_id_foreign` (`staff_id`),
  KEY `assets_created_by_foreign` (`created_by`),
  KEY `assets_updated_by_foreign` (`updated_by`),
  CONSTRAINT `assets_created_by_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`created_by`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `assets_staff_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`staff_id`) REFERENCES `staff` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `assets_updated_by_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`updated_by`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `assets_vehicle_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`vehicle_id`) REFERENCES `vehicles` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `incident_additional_services`;

  `amount` decimal(15,2) NOT NULL,
  `note` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `incident_additional_services_incident_id_foreign` (`incident_id`),
  KEY `incident_additional_services_additional_service_id_foreign` (`additional_service_id`),

  CONSTRAINT `incident_additional_services_incident_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`incident_id`) REFERENCES `incidents` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;


DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `incident_staff`;
CREATE TABLE `incident_staff` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `incident_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `staff_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `role` enum('driver','medical_staff') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `wage_amount` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Tin cng nhn vin cho chuyn i ny',
  `wage_details` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_bin COMMENT 'Chi tit cc loi tin cng (cng, thng, hoa hng, tip...)',
  `notes` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `incident_staff_incident_id_staff_id_role_unique` (`incident_id`,`staff_id`,`role`),
  KEY `incident_staff_incident_id_index` (`incident_id`),
  KEY `incident_staff_staff_id_index` (`staff_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `incident_staff_incident_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`incident_id`) REFERENCES `incidents` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `incident_staff_staff_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`staff_id`) REFERENCES `staff` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `incident_staff_chk_1` CHECK (json_valid(`wage_details`))
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `incidents`;
CREATE TABLE `incidents` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `vehicle_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `patient_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `date` datetime NOT NULL,
  `dispatch_by` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `destination` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `from_location_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `to_location_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `partner_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `commission_amount` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT NULL,
  `summary` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `tags` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_bin,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `incidents_dispatch_by_foreign` (`dispatch_by`),
  KEY `incidents_vehicle_id_index` (`vehicle_id`),
  KEY `incidents_patient_id_index` (`patient_id`),
  KEY `incidents_date_index` (`date`),
  KEY `incidents_vehicle_id_date_index` (`vehicle_id`,`date`),
  KEY `incidents_from_location_id_foreign` (`from_location_id`),
  KEY `incidents_to_location_id_foreign` (`to_location_id`),
  KEY `incidents_partner_id_foreign` (`partner_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `incidents_dispatch_by_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`dispatch_by`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `incidents_from_location_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`from_location_id`) REFERENCES `locations` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `incidents_partner_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`partner_id`) REFERENCES `partners` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `incidents_patient_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`patient_id`) REFERENCES `patients` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `incidents_to_location_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`to_location_id`) REFERENCES `locations` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `incidents_vehicle_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`vehicle_id`) REFERENCES `vehicles` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `incidents_chk_1` CHECK (json_valid(`tags`))
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `loan_interest_adjustments`;
CREATE TABLE `loan_interest_adjustments` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `loan_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `old_interest_rate` decimal(5,2) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Li sut c (%/nm)',
  `new_interest_rate` decimal(5,2) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Li sut mi (%/nm)',
  `effective_date` date NOT NULL COMMENT 'Ngy p dng',
  `note` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `created_by` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `loan_interest_adjustments_created_by_foreign` (`created_by`),
  KEY `loan_interest_adjustments_loan_id_effective_date_index` (`loan_id`,`effective_date`),
  CONSTRAINT `loan_interest_adjustments_created_by_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`created_by`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `loan_interest_adjustments_loan_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`loan_id`) REFERENCES `loan_profiles` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `loan_payment_history`;
CREATE TABLE `loan_payment_history` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `transaction_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `loan_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `payment_type` enum('regular','partial_prepayment','full_payoff') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `amount` decimal(15,2) NOT NULL,
  `schedules_snapshot` json NOT NULL COMMENT 'Snapshot of schedules before payment',
  `previous_remaining_balance` decimal(15,2) NOT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `loan_payment_history_transaction_id_foreign` (`transaction_id`),
  KEY `loan_payment_history_loan_id_foreign` (`loan_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `loan_payment_history_loan_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`loan_id`) REFERENCES `loan_profiles` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `loan_payment_history_transaction_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`transaction_id`) REFERENCES `transactions` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;


DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `loan_profiles`;
CREATE TABLE `loan_profiles` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `vehicle_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `cif` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'M h s khch hng',
  `contract_number` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'S hp ng tn dng',
  `bank_name` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'Tn ngn hng',
  `principal_amount` decimal(15,2) NOT NULL COMMENT 'S tin vay',
  `term_months` int NOT NULL COMMENT 'K hn (thng)',
  `total_periods` int NOT NULL COMMENT 'S k tr n',
  `disbursement_date` date NOT NULL COMMENT 'Ngy gii ngn',
  `base_interest_rate` decimal(5,2) NOT NULL COMMENT 'Li sut theo hp ng (%/nm)',
  `payment_day` tinyint NOT NULL COMMENT 'Ngy tr n hng thng (1-28)',
  `first_period_interest_only` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0' COMMENT 'K u tin ch tr li, khng tr gc',
  `status` enum('active','paid_off','cancelled') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'active',
  `remaining_balance` decimal(15,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT 'D n cn li',
  `note` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `created_by` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_by` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `loan_profiles_created_by_foreign` (`created_by`),
  KEY `loan_profiles_updated_by_foreign` (`updated_by`),
  KEY `loan_profiles_vehicle_id_status_index` (`vehicle_id`,`status`),
  CONSTRAINT `loan_profiles_created_by_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`created_by`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `loan_profiles_updated_by_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`updated_by`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `loan_profiles_vehicle_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`vehicle_id`) REFERENCES `vehicles` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `locations`;
CREATE TABLE `locations` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `type` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'both',
  `address` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `note` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `is_active` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `locations_name_index` (`name`),
  KEY `locations_type_index` (`type`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `media`;
CREATE TABLE `media` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `model_type` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `model_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `uuid` char(36) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `collection_name` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `file_name` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `mime_type` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `disk` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `conversions_disk` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `size` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `manipulations` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_bin NOT NULL,
  `custom_properties` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_bin NOT NULL,
  `generated_conversions` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_bin NOT NULL,
  `responsive_images` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_bin NOT NULL,
  `order_column` int unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `media_uuid_unique` (`uuid`),
  KEY `media_model_type_model_id_index` (`model_type`,`model_id`),
  KEY `media_order_column_index` (`order_column`),
  CONSTRAINT `media_chk_1` CHECK (json_valid(`manipulations`)),
  CONSTRAINT `media_chk_2` CHECK (json_valid(`custom_properties`)),
  CONSTRAINT `media_chk_3` CHECK (json_valid(`generated_conversions`)),
  CONSTRAINT `media_chk_4` CHECK (json_valid(`responsive_images`))
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `notes`;
CREATE TABLE `notes` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `incident_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `vehicle_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `user_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `note` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `severity` enum('info','warning','critical') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'info',
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `notes_user_id_foreign` (`user_id`),
  KEY `notes_incident_id_index` (`incident_id`),
  KEY `notes_vehicle_id_index` (`vehicle_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `notes_incident_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`incident_id`) REFERENCES `incidents` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `notes_user_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`user_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `notes_vehicle_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`vehicle_id`) REFERENCES `vehicles` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `password_reset_tokens`;
CREATE TABLE `password_reset_tokens` (
  `email` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `token` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`email`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;


DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `patients`;
CREATE TABLE `patients` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `birth_year` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `phone` varchar(20) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `gender` enum('male','female','other') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `address` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `notes` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `patients_name_index` (`name`),
  KEY `patients_phone_index` (`phone`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `personal_access_tokens`;
CREATE TABLE `personal_access_tokens` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `tokenable_type` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `tokenable_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `name` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `token` varchar(64) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `abilities` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `last_used_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `expires_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `personal_access_tokens_token_unique` (`token`),
  KEY `personal_access_tokens_tokenable_type_tokenable_id_index` (`tokenable_type`,`tokenable_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `salary_advances`;
CREATE TABLE `salary_advances` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `staff_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `amount` decimal(15,2) NOT NULL,
  `from_earnings` decimal(15,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `from_company` decimal(15,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `debt_amount` decimal(15,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00',
  `status` enum('pending','approved','paid_off') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'approved',
  `note` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `transaction_ids` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_bin,
  `approved_by` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `approved_at` datetime DEFAULT NULL,
  `date` datetime NOT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `salary_advances_approved_by_foreign` (`approved_by`),
  KEY `salary_advances_staff_id_index` (`staff_id`),
  KEY `salary_advances_status_index` (`status`),
  KEY `salary_advances_date_index` (`date`),
  CONSTRAINT `salary_advances_approved_by_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`approved_by`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `salary_advances_staff_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`staff_id`) REFERENCES `staff` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `salary_advances_chk_1` CHECK (json_valid(`transaction_ids`))
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;


DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `staff`;
CREATE TABLE `staff` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `user_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `full_name` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `employee_code` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `staff_type` enum('medical_staff','driver','manager','investor','admin','vehicle_owner') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'medical_staff',
  `equity_percentage` decimal(5,2) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'T l vn gp (%) - ch p dng cho c ng',
  `vehicle_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `phone` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `email` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `id_card` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `birth_date` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `gender` enum('male','female','other') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `address` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `hire_date` date DEFAULT NULL,
  `department` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `position` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `base_salary` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Lng c bn hng thng',
  `notes` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `is_active` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `staff_employee_code_unique` (`employee_code`),
  KEY `staff_user_id_foreign` (`user_id`),
  KEY `staff_vehicle_id_foreign` (`vehicle_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `staff_user_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`user_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `staff_vehicle_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`vehicle_id`) REFERENCES `vehicles` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `staff_adjustments`;
CREATE TABLE `staff_adjustments` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `staff_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `incident_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_by` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `type` enum('addition','deduction') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'addition = cng, deduction = tr',
  `amount` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL,
  `month` date NOT NULL COMMENT 'Thng p dng iu chnh (YYYY-MM-01)',
  `category` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'Loi: thng, pht, tm ng, etc',
  `reason` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT 'L do iu chnh',
  `status` enum('pending','applied','debt') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending' COMMENT 'pending = ch, applied =  p dng, debt = n',
  `debt_amount` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT 'S tin n nu khng  tr',
  `applied_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Thi im p dng',
  `transaction_ids` longtext CHARACTER SET utf8mb4 COLLATE utf8mb4_bin COMMENT 'Danh sch ID transactions c to',
  `from_incident_amount` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT 'S tin ly t chuyn i',
  `from_company_amount` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT 'S tin ly t cng ty',
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `staff_adjustments_created_by_foreign` (`created_by`),
  KEY `staff_adjustments_staff_id_month_index` (`staff_id`,`month`),
  KEY `staff_adjustments_status_index` (`status`),
  KEY `staff_adjustments_incident_id_foreign` (`incident_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `staff_adjustments_created_by_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`created_by`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `staff_adjustments_incident_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`incident_id`) REFERENCES `incidents` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `staff_adjustments_staff_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`staff_id`) REFERENCES `staff` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `staff_adjustments_chk_1` CHECK (json_valid(`transaction_ids`))
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

  `value` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,

  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,

  UNIQUE KEY `system_settings_key_unique` (`key`),
  KEY `system_settings_group_index` (`group`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `transactions`;
CREATE TABLE `transactions` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `code` varchar(20) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `incident_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `staff_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `vehicle_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `vehicle_maintenance_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `type` enum('thu','chi','du_kien_chi','nop_quy','vay_cong_ty','tra_cong_ty') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `category` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `transaction_category` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'thu_chinh, chi_chinh, tien_cong_lai_xe, tien_cong_nvyt, hoa_hong, bao_tri, dich_vu_bo_sung, chi_phi_bo_sung',
  `is_active` tinyint(1) NOT NULL DEFAULT '1',
  `replaced_by` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `edited_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `edited_by` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `amount` decimal(15,2) NOT NULL,
  `method` enum('cash','bank','other') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'cash',
  `payment_method` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `note` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `from_account` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Ti khon ngun',
  `to_account` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Ti khon ch',
  `from_balance_before` decimal(15,2) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'S d ti khon ngun trc GD',
  `from_balance_after` decimal(15,2) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'S d ti khon ngun sau GD',
  `to_balance_before` decimal(15,2) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'S d ti khon ch trc GD',
  `to_balance_after` decimal(15,2) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'S d ti khon ch sau GD',
  `recorded_by` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `date` datetime NOT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `transactions_code_unique` (`code`),
  KEY `transactions_recorded_by_foreign` (`recorded_by`),
  KEY `transactions_incident_id_index` (`incident_id`),
  KEY `transactions_vehicle_id_index` (`vehicle_id`),
  KEY `transactions_type_index` (`type`),
  KEY `transactions_date_index` (`date`),
  KEY `transactions_vehicle_id_type_date_index` (`vehicle_id`,`type`,`date`),
  KEY `transactions_staff_id_index` (`staff_id`),
  KEY `transactions_category_index` (`category`),
  KEY `transactions_vehicle_maintenance_id_foreign` (`vehicle_maintenance_id`),
  KEY `transactions_replaced_by_foreign` (`replaced_by`),
  KEY `transactions_edited_by_foreign` (`edited_by`),
  KEY `transactions_transaction_category_index` (`transaction_category`),
  KEY `transactions_is_active_index` (`is_active`),
  KEY `transactions_code_index` (`code`),
  CONSTRAINT `transactions_edited_by_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`edited_by`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `transactions_incident_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`incident_id`) REFERENCES `incidents` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `transactions_recorded_by_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`recorded_by`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`),
  CONSTRAINT `transactions_replaced_by_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`replaced_by`) REFERENCES `transactions` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `transactions_staff_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`staff_id`) REFERENCES `staff` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `transactions_vehicle_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`vehicle_id`) REFERENCES `vehicles` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `transactions_vehicle_maintenance_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`vehicle_maintenance_id`) REFERENCES `vehicle_maintenances` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `users`;
CREATE TABLE `users` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `name` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `email` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `email_verified_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `password` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `remember_token` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `users_email_unique` (`email`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `vehicle_maintenances`;
CREATE TABLE `vehicle_maintenances` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `vehicle_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `maintenance_service_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `partner_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `incident_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `user_id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL,
  `date` date NOT NULL,
  `cost` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL,
  `mileage` int DEFAULT NULL,
  `description` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `note` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `vehicle_maintenances_maintenance_service_id_foreign` (`maintenance_service_id`),
  KEY `vehicle_maintenances_partner_id_foreign` (`partner_id`),
  KEY `vehicle_maintenances_incident_id_foreign` (`incident_id`),
  KEY `vehicle_maintenances_user_id_foreign` (`user_id`),
  KEY `vehicle_maintenances_vehicle_id_index` (`vehicle_id`),
  KEY `vehicle_maintenances_date_index` (`date`),
  CONSTRAINT `vehicle_maintenances_incident_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`incident_id`) REFERENCES `incidents` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `vehicle_maintenances_maintenance_service_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`maintenance_service_id`) REFERENCES `maintenance_services` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `vehicle_maintenances_partner_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`partner_id`) REFERENCES `partners` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  CONSTRAINT `vehicle_maintenances_user_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`user_id`) REFERENCES `users` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `vehicle_maintenances_vehicle_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`vehicle_id`) REFERENCES `vehicles` (`id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `vehicles`;
CREATE TABLE `vehicles` (
  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `license_plate` varchar(20) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL,
  `model` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `driver_name` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `driver_id` bigint unsigned DEFAULT NULL,
  `phone` varchar(20) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL,
  `status` enum('active','inactive','maintenance') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL DEFAULT 'active',
  `note` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci,
  `created_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  `updated_at` timestamp NULL DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `vehicles_license_plate_unique` (`license_plate`),
  KEY `vehicles_license_plate_index` (`license_plate`),
  KEY `vehicles_driver_id_foreign` (`driver_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `vehicles_driver_id_foreign` FOREIGN KEY (`driver_id`) REFERENCES `staff` (`id`) ON DELETE SET NULL
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;

  `id` bigint unsigned NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,

) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci;
